alias (sBidBlocks, mBidBlocks);
*pEnergyBidSize(sResources,sBidBlocks,sTimePeriods)$(ord(sBidBlocks)>1 and pEnergyBidSize(sResources,sBidBlocks,sTimePeriods) > 0.0001) = pEnergyBidSize(sResources,sBidBlocks,sTimePeriods) - sum(mBidBlocks$(ord(mBidBlocks)>=1), pEnergyBidSize(sResources,mBidBlocks,sTimePeriods)$(ord(mBidBlocks)<ord(sBidBlocks)));
pEnergyBidSize(sResources,sBidBlocks,sTimePeriods)$((pResourceType(sResources) = GEN or pResourceType(sResources) = LOAD ) and ord(sBidBlocks)>1 and pEnergyBidSize(sResources,sBidBlocks,sTimePeriods) > 0.0001) = pEnergyBidSize(sResources,sBidBlocks,sTimePeriods) -  pEnergyBidSize(sResources,sBidBlocks-1,sTimePeriods);

display pEnergyBidSize;
